## [Unreleased]

### Changed

- **Perf: batchowane idempotency-checki + `createMany` na hot-pathach (audyt perf)** **(#748)** â€” z autonomicznego audytu wydajnoإ›ci (agent przeskanowaإ‚ 192 trasy `api/**` + `lib/`). **2أ— N+1 â†’ jeden batch:** ingestiony cronأ³w robiإ‚y `findUnique` **per wiersz** w pؤ™tli przeciw puli `max:3`: `lib/streamlabs.ts` (poll donejtأ³w â€” do 50 point-readأ³w/cykl **przed** jakؤ…kolwiek pracؤ…) i `app/api/yt/poll-live-chat` (kaإ¼da wiadomoإ›ؤ‡ live-chatu, w tym zwykإ‚e teksty logowane do `youTubeEvent`) â†’ teraz **jeden `findMany({ externalId/messageId: { in } })` + `Set`** przed pؤ™tlؤ… (oba klucze `@unique`; `Set.add` w pؤ™tli pilnuje braku podwأ³jnej insercji w obrؤ™bie batcha â€” parytet ze starym per-row check). **2أ— `createMany` w `$transaction`:** powiadomienia przegranych w `resolvePrediction` (`lib/predictions.ts`) i wspierajؤ…cych/zwrotأ³w w `resolveBounty` (`lib/bounties.ts`) wstawiane byإ‚y **po jednym `create`** w pؤ™tli, trzymajؤ…c poإ‚ؤ…czenie tx tym dإ‚uإ¼ej, im wiؤ™cej obstawiajؤ…cych/backerأ³w; ruch GT (`user.update`/`transaction.create`) **zostaje per-wiersz** (musi), same powiadomienia â†’ jeden `createMany` (skraca sekcjؤ™ krytycznؤ…). **Behavior-preserving** (identyczne wiersze, te same إ›cieإ¼ki, guard `length>0`). Towarzyszؤ…cy **audyt cross-tenant** (agent, 76 tras admina) â€” **czysty**, izolacja solidna; jedyna uwaga: `AdminAction` (log audytu) jest globalny z zaإ‚oإ¼enia â†’ osobny follow-up (kolumna `tenantId`+backfill = db push, do decyzji). Bez db push / schematu / nowych testأ³w (إ›cieإ¼ki I/O). Zielone: tsc/641 testأ³w/eslint/build/docs:check.

- **White-label: przycisk â€‍Premium" w nagإ‚أ³wku ukryty przed widzami sub-portali (zgإ‚oszone przez wإ‚aإ›ciciela)** **(#746)** â€” zإ‚oty CTA â€‍âœ¨ Premium" (#744) renderowaإ‚ siؤ™ w nagإ‚أ³wku **bezwarunkowo na kaإ¼dym portalu**, wiؤ™c widzowie i goإ›cie na white-labelowym sub-portalu streamera widzieli upsell **planu SaaS platformy** â€” bez sensu (to streamer kupuje Premium dla SWOJEGO portalu, nie jego widzowie). Teraz CTA jest bramkowany: **marki storefrontu platformy** (portal-zaإ‚oإ¼yciel **oraz** publiczna marka E-Forge na empire-forge.com) pokazujؤ… go wszystkim (lejek sprzedaإ¼owy), a **sub-portal streamera** â€” tylko jego **adminowi** (ktأ³ry realnie moإ¼e podnieإ›ؤ‡ plan swojego portalu przez `/api/billing/checkout`, scoped po `ownerUserId`); widzowie/goإ›cie go nie dostajؤ…. Nowy pure helper **`isPlatformBrand(tenant)`** (`lib/tenant.ts`) = `isFounderBrand(t) || t.ownerUserId == null` â€” unia إ‚apie **obie** marki platformy (zaإ‚oإ¼yciel ma `ownerUserId`, ale jest founder-slugiem; e-forge nie jest founderem, ale ma `ownerUserId=null`), a przyszإ‚e portale streamerأ³w (z onboardingu â†’ majؤ… `ownerUserId` i nie sؤ… founderem) wypadajؤ… â†’ tam Premium tylko dla admina. Flaga niesiona do klienta jako **boolean** w `TenantBranding` (`ownerUserId` zostaje server-side, bez wycieku id). **Brak efektu w prod dziإ›** â€” oba istniejؤ…ce portale to marki platformy (zweryfikowane na إ¼ywej bazie: `ghost-empire` founder-slug, `e-forge` `ownerUserId=null`), wiؤ™c przycisk pokazuje siؤ™ jak dotؤ…d; to poprawnoإ›ؤ‡ na przyszإ‚oإ›ؤ‡, gdy powstanؤ… sub-portale. Tour nietkniؤ™ty (krok â€‍premium" nie istnieje w jego stepach, a brakujؤ…ce cele i tak sؤ… pomijane). Zweryfikowane renderem na إ¼ywo (founder-brand: link â€‍Premium" obecny i widoczny, brak regresji; konsola czysta poza znanym dev-mode CSP-eval). Bez db push / schematu / nowych testأ³w (logika pure, spأ³jna z nietestowanym `isFounderBrand`). Zielone: tsc/641 testأ³w/eslint/build/docs:check.

- **Dekompozycja: lazy-importy sekcji wyniesione z `AdminClient` (na إ¼yczenie wإ‚aإ›ciciela â€‍zrأ³b dekompozycjؤ™")** **(#736)** â€” `AdminClient.tsx` **936 â†’ 878 l.**: blok **63 `dynamic()` lazy-importأ³w sekcji** + `SectionLoading` przeniesiony do nowego **`admin/lazy-sections.tsx`** (zero sprzؤ™إ¼enia typأ³w â€” najczystszy szew z caإ‚ej szأ³stki; importy sؤ… niezaleإ¼nymi module-level staإ‚ymi). **Empiryczna obserwacja (dlaczego tylko AdminClient):** prأ³ba analogicznego splitu `ProfileClient` (1017 l.) daإ‚a **56 nieuإ¼ywanych importأ³w + sprzؤ™إ¼enie typu `Props`** â€” jego sub-komponenty (StatTile/SocialLinksEditor/AccountsAndLinksâ€¦) wspأ³إ‚dzielؤ… powierzchniؤ™ importأ³w i typy gإ‚أ³wnego komponentu, wiؤ™c podziaإ‚ tworzy **duplikacjؤ™ importأ³w bez zysku** (gorszy kod) â€” **cofniؤ™te**. - **CSP: `unsafe-inline` usuniؤ™te ze `style-src` (przeniesione do `style-src-attr`) + ekstrakcja inline `<style>` (na إ¼yczenie wإ‚aإ›ciciela)** **(#735)** â€” utwardzenie odroczone z audytu, doprowadzone tak daleko, jak pozwala spec CSP. **Wszystkie 30 inline blokأ³w `<style>` wyniesione** do CSS إ‚adowanego przez `<link>` (`'self'`): keyframe'y (casino `gefx-*`, toast `getoastin`, overlaye `gesp-in`/`gegoal-shimmer`/`geqr-in`/`wheelPop`/`gerevealin`/`ge-combo-*`) â†’ **`globals.css`**; **22 zduplikowane resety OBS** (`html,body{transparent}` â€¦) â†’ jeden **`overlay/overlay.css`** importowany raz w `overlay/layout.tsx` (przy okazji kasuje duplikacjؤ™ أ—22). Dziؤ™ki temu CSP rozdzielone: **`style-src 'self' https://fonts.googleapis.com`** (elementy/`<style>` â€” **bez `unsafe-inline`**) + **`style-src-attr 'unsafe-inline'`** (konieczne dla ~638 dynamicznych inline `style={{}}` â€” nonce/hash CSP **nie obejmujؤ… atrybutأ³w stylu**, a wartoإ›ci sؤ… runtime-dynamiczne). **Zweryfikowane na إ¼ywo:** nagإ‚أ³wek CSP = `style-src 'self' â€¦` (zero `unsafe-inline`) + `style-src-attr 'unsafe-inline'`; **0 blokأ³w `<style>` w HTML**; overlay `/overlay/wheel` body = **transparent** (`rgba(0,0,0,0)`, reset z overlay.css) + `min-height:0`; **wszystkie keyframe'y obecne globalnie** (8/8 sprawdzonych, animacje dziaإ‚ajؤ…); inline-atrybuty stylu nadal aplikowane; **brak** â€‍Refused to apply inline style". Bez zmiany schematu/testأ³w. Zielone: tsc/622 testأ³w/eslint/build/docs:check.

- **React Compiler: wإ‚ؤ…czenie reguإ‚ `purity`/`refs`/`immutability` (na إ¼yczenie wإ‚aإ›ciciela â€‍zrأ³b odroczone")** **(#734)** â€” wykonanie tego, co #733 odإ‚oإ¼yإ‚o. Z 110 ostrzeإ¼eإ„ 12 niesetstate'owych (5 purity + 5 immutability + 2 refs) **rozwiؤ…zane**, dziؤ™ki czemu te **3 reguإ‚y sؤ… teraz EGZEKWOWANE** (`error`) â€” nowe naruszenia blokujؤ… lint. Rozwiؤ…zanie = **2 realne fixy strukturalne** + **9 celowych inline-disable** na legalnie-flagowanych miejscach: (fixy) `lib/use-focus-trap.ts` â€” zapis â€‍latest ref" przeniesiony z renderu do `useEffect`; `overlay/OverlayClient.tsx` â€” samowywoإ‚ujؤ…cy siؤ™ `useCallback` (alert-loop) przepiؤ™ty na wzorzec `showNextRef.current()` (ref deklarowany przed callbackiem, sync w efekcie) â†’ koniec â€‍access before declaration"; (disable z uzasadnieniem) `Date.now()` w **serwerowym** `events/page.tsx` (request-time, poprawne), `Date.now()` w **handlerach** (`SceneBuilder` unikalne id), render-time `Date.now()` dla **nie-tykajؤ…cych** wyإ›wietlaczy (`SeasonsClient` dni, admin `Subathon` preview), **إ¼ywy drift-corrected countdown** (`SubathonOverlayClient` â€” czyta Date.now()+ref co tick **z zaإ‚oإ¼enia**), mutacje DOM/cookie/nawigacja w **click-handlerach** (`ThemeToggle`, `OnboardingClient`, `ProfileClient`). **`set-state-in-effect` zostaje OFF** (98أ— idiomatyczny client data-fetching â€” patrz #733; wإ‚ؤ…czenie = 98 disable/architektura, zero zysku). Zweryfikowane: eslint 0 bإ‚ؤ™dأ³w (3 reguإ‚y czyste), render `/overlay` + `/overlay/subathon` 200 bez bإ‚ؤ™dأ³w runtime (self-ref OK). Bez zmiany schematu/testأ³w. Zielone: tsc/622 testأ³w/eslint/build/docs:check.

- **Rozpatrzenie pozostaإ‚ych pozycji â€‍odroczonych" z audytu â€” React Compiler + CSP + dekompozycja** **(#733)** â€” domkniؤ™cie `AUDIT_REPORT.md آ§0` analizؤ… zamiast إ›lepego churnu. **(1) ~101 ostrzeإ¼eإ„ React Compiler â†’ ZOSTAJؤ„ OFF (poprawna decyzja).** Zweryfikowane lokalnie (reguإ‚y wإ‚ؤ…czone): **110 = 98 `set-state-in-effect` + 5 purity + 5 immutability + 2 refs**. 98 to standardowy client-side **data-fetching** (`useEffect(()=>apiGet().then(setState))`); kompilator (ON) bezpiecznie **bailuje** (nigdy nie miskompiluje). â€‍Naprawa" = migracja kaإ¼dego fetcha do RSC/SWR (zmiana architektury) lub 98 inline-disable (gorzej niإ¼ config) â€” zero zysku poprawnoإ›ciowego, realne ryzyko regresji. Komentarz w `eslint.config.mjs` doprecyzowany zweryfikowanymi liczbami. **(2) CSP `style-src 'unsafe-inline'` â†’ ZOSTAJE (konieczny trade-off).** Zweryfikowane: **638 inline `style={{}}` w 142 plikach + 31 blokأ³w `<style>`**. CSP nonce/hash obejmuje tylko `<style>` **elementy**, nigdy inline-`style=` **atrybuty**, a wartoإ›ci sؤ… dynamiczne (nie do zahashowania) â†’ usuniؤ™cie niewykonalne bez zإ‚amania overlayأ³w/animacji/paskأ³w. Ryzyko CSS-injection niskie, a `script-src` jest juإ¼ ciasne (nonce + strict-dynamic, **bez** unsafe-inline/unsafe-eval â€” tam jest realna ochrona XSS). Rationale dopisane w `proxy.ts`. **(3) Dekompozycja pozostaإ‚ych 6 komponentأ³w 600+ l. â†’ NIE robiona (analiza strukturalna).** W odrأ³إ¼nieniu od `KasynoClient` (#732, kolekcja ~15 niezaleإ¼nych sub-komponentأ³w â†’ czysty podziaإ‚), te sؤ… **spأ³jne/stanowe** (np. `RankingClient` 5 decl/9 hookأ³w = jeden komponent; `AdminClient` 72 decl â‰ˆ **51 lazy-importأ³w** = sekcje juإ¼ wydzielone). Rozmiar = nieodإ‚ؤ…czna logika renderu ze wspأ³إ‚dzielonymi danymi â†’ podziaإ‚ wymusiإ‚by **prop-drilling** (gorszy smell) bez zysku. Heurystyka â€‍>600 l." nie wskazuje tu dإ‚ugu; robiؤ‡ chirurgicznie przy nastؤ™pnym dotkniؤ™ciu. **Bez zmiany zachowania / schematu / testأ³w** (tylko komentarze + dokumentacja). - **Admin i18n + a11y: 15 surowych etykiet â†’ klucze + bezimienne kontrolki (audyt admina)** **(#749)** â€” z autonomicznego audytu panelu (agent przeskanowaإ‚ ~51 sekcji + shell). **i18n (surowy angielski u polskiego admina), 7 sekcji:** `CreateDrop` (`Reward/Bonus {sym}`, `Bonus slots`), `Seasons` (Tier/Label/Value/Premium track), `StreamGoals` (Reset/Target), `Subathon` (Start/Stop), `Streamlabs` (toast â€‍Sync: fetchedâ€¦" + â€‍Sync now"), `YouTubeLive` (â€‍Poll now"), `Predictions` (â€‍âœ“ Win") â€” wszystkie przepiؤ™te na `t()`. **a11y, 3 sekcje:** `PaymentMethods` â€” ikonkowe przyciski zmiany kolejnoإ›ci â†‘/â†“ dostaإ‚y `title` (move up/down); `ActiveDrops` + `Schedule` â€” ikonkowe `Trash2` dostaإ‚y `title` (delete) â€” dotؤ…d bezimienne dla czytnika ekranu. i18n **+19 kluczy** w 10 namespace'ach `admin.*` EN+PL (`deleteTitle` jest **per-namespace** â€” nie istniaإ‚ w `activeDrops`/`schedule`, wiؤ™c dodany, nie reuse); dodane chirurgicznie skryptem node (CRLF, kotwica 4-spacjowa `\r\n    "<ns>"` omija top-level namespace'y `seasons`/`predictions`/`schedule` o tej samej nazwie, diff addytywny 38/0). **Zweryfikowane na إ¼ywo** (tymczasowa publiczna strona rozwiؤ…zujؤ…ca wszystkie 19 kluczy, potem usuniؤ™ta): `/en`+`/pl` renderujؤ… poprawnie, **ICU params podstawione** (â€‍Reward GT", â€‍Synchronizacja: pobrano 1, dopasowano 2â€¦"), zero `MISSING_MESSAGE`. - **i18n + a11y: zlokalizowane strony 404/bإ‚ؤ™du dla widzأ³w + drobne braki a11y (audyt autonomiczny)** **(#747)** â€” sweep najإ›wieإ¼szych powierzchni widza (po #746) dwoma agentami audytowymi. **Bug i18n (realny, white-label):** `[locale]/not-found.tsx` (404) i `[locale]/error.tsx` (granica bإ‚ؤ™du trasy) byإ‚y **w 100% zahardkodowane po polsku** â€” anglo/niemiecko/â€¦-jؤ™zyczna widownia streamera widziaإ‚a polskie strony systemowe na **kaإ¼dym** locale. - **Podglؤ…d `/support` w panelu Pإ‚atnoإ›ci nie renderowaإ‚ siؤ™ â€” CSP `frame-ancestors 'none'`** **(#728)** â€” zgإ‚oszone przez wإ‚aإ›ciciela: â€‍Podglؤ…d na إ¼ywo â€“ strona /support" w sekcji Pإ‚atnoإ›ci pokazywaإ‚ **pustؤ…/zepsutؤ… ramkؤ™** (ikona â€‍nie moإ¼na wyإ›wietliؤ‡") zamiast strony. Zmienione na **`frame-ancestors 'self'`** â€” portal moإ¼e osadzaؤ‡ **wإ‚asne** strony (podglؤ…d /support), a osadzanie z **obcych** domen (clickjacking) **pozostaje zablokowane**. Zweryfikowane na إ¼ywo: nagإ‚أ³wek CSP na `/support` = `frame-ancestors 'self'`, **brak** bإ‚ؤ™du â€‍Refused to display â€¦ frame-ancestors" w konsoli, `/support` renderuje treإ›ؤ‡ (516 znakأ³w UI). Zielone: tsc/618 testأ³w/eslint/build/docs:check.

- **Bإ‚ؤ…d ICU `UNCLOSED_TAG` na stronie logowania (`<provider>` w 14 lokalizacjach)** **(#727)** â€” wykryty podczas peإ‚nej weryfikacji platformy. Naprawione we **wszystkich 14 lokalizacjach** (`<provider>` â†’ ICU-safe `[provider]`); skan caإ‚ego katalogu i18n potwierdziإ‚ **brak innych** nieذ·ذ°ذ¼kniؤ™tych tagأ³w. Zielone: tsc/618 testأ³w/eslint/build/docs:check.

- **Extract achievement-progress logic to a tested shared lib (audit v5 quality)** **(#648)** â€” the `/achievements` progress bars ("Level 8/10" toward a locked achievement) already worked, but the math lived **inline + untested** in `AchievementsClient` (`getProgress`). Extracted it to a pure **`lib/achievement-progress`** (`achievementProgress(triggerType, triggerValue, stats)` â†’ `{current,target,pct}` or null for manual/dynamic/logged-out) and wired the client to it â€” behaviour-identical (rounded `pct` vs the old floored ratio = â‰¤1% display diff). Adds **+4 tests â†’ 477** covering the triggerâ†’stat mapping, the 100% cap and the null cases that were previously uncovered. No UI/behaviour change. Zielone: `tsc`/**477 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **Dependency batch-bump â€” all safe patch/minor in-range (audit v4 hygiene)** **(#640)** â€” `npm update` within the existing `^` ranges: **next/eslint-config-next/@next/bundle-analyzer 16.2.7 â†’ 16.2.9**, **@sentry/nextjs 10.56 â†’ 10.59**, **stripe 22.2.0 â†’ 22.2.2**, **pg 8.21 â†’ 8.22**, **tailwindcss + @tailwindcss/postcss 4.3.0 â†’ 4.3.1**, **vitest 4.1.8 â†’ 4.1.9**, **lucide-react 1.17 â†’ 1.21**, **@playwright/test 1.60 â†’ 1.61**, **@types/node â†’ 25.9.4**. - **Composite `[tenantId, <sort>]` indexes for per-tenant leaderboards (audit v4 perf)** **(#638)** â€” the ranking/top-users reads filter by `tenantId` **then** sort by `tokens`/`totalEarned`/`level,xp`/`streak`, which a lone single-column index can't fully serve (Postgres picks one â†’ filter+sort). Added `User @@index([tenantId, tokens])`, `[tenantId, totalEarned]`, `[tenantId, level, xp]`, `[tenantId, streak]` so each portal's board is a pure index range scan. **db push** â€” purely additive (CREATE INDEX), applied. Bounded today by the 45 s ranking cache, but prevents degradation as tenants/users grow. Single-column indexes kept for the global/legacy sort. Zielone: `tsc`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **`/polls` and `/predictions` tally via `groupBy` instead of loading every row (audit v4 perf)** **(#635)** â€” both public pages loaded **all** vote/entry rows and counted in JS: `/polls` pulled every `PollVote` for 30 polls each render; `/predictions` pulled every `PredictionEntry` (unbounded) for active predictions to sum wagers. A popular poll/prediction made these heavy index-less reads on every page load. Now both use DB aggregation (`pollVote.groupBy [pollId,optionIndex] _count`; `predictionEntry.groupBy [predictionId,optionIndex] _sum+_count`) + a small scoped fetch of only the viewer's own votes/entries â€” exactly what the OBS overlay feeds already did. Output payload shape is byte-identical, so the client components are unchanged. Index-backed (`[pollId,optionIndex]`, `[predictionId,optionIndex]` exist). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **Donation poll every 15 min instead of once a day (audit v4 perf)** **(#634)** â€” `/api/cron/streamlabs-poll` ran `0 6 * * *` (once daily), so a Streamlabs donation could wait **up to ~24h** before crediting GT + firing the thank-you â€” brutal for a live-stream economy. Now `*/15 * * * *` (every 15 min). The handler is cheap and idempotent (dedup via `Donation.externalId @unique`), so the higher cadence can't double-credit. Requires Vercel **Pro** (sub-daily crons) â€” confirmed by the owner. Config-only. Zielone: `build`/`docs:check`.

- **Vercel deploy wywalaإ‚ siؤ™ od #629 â€” produkcja zamroإ¼ona, `.npmrc` legacy-peer-deps** **(#654)** â€” **KRYTYCZNE:** produkcja staإ‚a na **#628** od bumpa `@simplewebauthn` 9â†’13 (#629). Vercel robi إ›wieإ¼e `npm install` (resolucja), ktأ³re padaإ‚o z **ERESOLVE**: `next-auth@5-beta` deklaruje opcjonalny peer `@simplewebauthn/browser@^9`, a projekt ma `^13`. Kaإ¼dy deploy #629â€“#653 â†’ `Error`, wiؤ™c caإ‚y dorobek (system ticketأ³w #649â€“#652, white-label #653 itd.) **byإ‚ w `main`, ale NIE na إ¼ywo**. Lokalne bramki tego nie إ‚apaإ‚y, bo uإ¼ywaإ‚y `npm ci` (odtwarza lockfile, bez re-resolucji) i `npx next build` â€” nie إ›wieإ¼ego `npm install`. Fix: **`ghost-empire-web/.npmrc` z `legacy-peer-deps=true`** (dokإ‚adnie to, co rekomenduje npm; peer jest *optional*, a v13 jest przetestowane i dziaإ‚a). Potwierdzone: `npm install --dry-run --legacy-peer-deps=false` reprodukuje ERESOLVE, z `.npmrc` przechodzi czysto. Odblokowuje deploy 25 commitأ³w. **Wniosek procesowy: dodaؤ‡ إ›wieإ¼e `npm install` do weryfikacji przed pushem.** Zielone: install-resolve OK + `tsc`/**483 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build --turbopack`/`docs:check` (z #653).

- **`/schedule` was hard-coded Polish + the founder's handle (audit v4 white-label)** **(#643)** â€” the public schedule page rendered a literal `PLAN STREAMأ“W` title, `Kiedy Gh0s77tt jest liveâ€¦` subtitle (the founder's handle baked in), a Polish empty-state, and hard-coded Polish weekday names â€” so non-PL visitors saw Polish and any other portal showed the founder's identity. Now title/subtitle/empty-state are i18n keys, the streamer name comes from `tenant.ownerHandle` (`{owner}` param), and weekday names reuse the localized `schedule.daysFull` array. EN + PL. (Per-tenant timezone is still a literal â€” a `Tenant.timezone` field is a separate future addition.) Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **Backend hygiene sweep (audit v4)** **(#642)** â€” three small server-side correctness fixes: (1) **duel** â€” the post-commit `checkAndGrantAchievements` is now `.catch()`-guarded, so a throw in best-effort side effects can never turn an already-paid, committed duel into a misleading error to the winner; (2) **shop** â€” creating a shop item logged the audit action as `create_drop` (a TODO); added a proper `create_shop_item` action and used it; (3) **crons** â€” all three Vercel-cron handlers (`streamlabs-poll`, `prune`, `weekly-rewards`) now verify `CRON_SECRET` in **constant time** via a new `verifyCronSecret` helper (parity with `verifyBotSecret`) instead of a timing-variable `!==`. No schema change, no db push. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **Game-sync hardening sweep (audit v4)** **(#641)** â€” four correctness fixes in the per-tenant library sync: (1) **PSN titles now key on the stable `npCommunicationId`** only â€” the old `|| trophyTitleName` fallback keyed on the display name, so a missing/changed name re-keyed the game as a new row, pruned the old one and **lost its GameVotes**; titles without a stable id are skipped. (2) **NaN-date guard on the PSN sync** (a malformed `lastUpdatedDateTime` would store `Invalid Date`) â€” same guard Xbox already had. (3) **The legacy null-tenant "land-grab" now runs only on the FIRST sync per platform** (gated by `steam/psn/xboxSyncedAt`) instead of every sync, so it can't repeatedly absorb another tenant's pre-backfill rows. (4) **`getGameLibraryConfig` is race-safe** â€” concurrent first-syncs that both `create` the per-tenant config (`tenantId @unique`) now catch P2002 and re-read instead of erroring. No schema change, no db push. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **Raffle ticket numbering race â†’ duplicate ticket numbers (audit v4)** **(#639)** â€” buying raffle tickets read `max(ticketNumber)+1` then `createMany`, all in a tx â€” but under READ COMMITTED two concurrent buyers could read the same max and mint **duplicate ticket numbers**, corrupting the draw (two holders of "ticket #42"). GT spend itself was always safe (`gte` guard). Fixed by **locking the event row** (`SELECT â€¦ FOR UPDATE`) at the top of the tx so per-raffle purchases serialize through the read-maxâ†’insert section (different raffles don't block each other); the per-user `maxTicketsPerUser` cap count is serialized for free too. No unique constraint added (would risk failing on any pre-existing dup), no schema change, no db push. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

### Security

- **RLS enablement runbook for Supabase (audit v5, defense-in-depth)** **(#647)** â€” new **`docs/RLS.md`**: a ready-to-paste SQL block that enables Row-Level Security on all 95 `public` tables, closing the **anon/PostgREST** exposure (a leaked anon key can't read tables over the auto-generated REST API) while leaving the **Prisma app unaffected** (it connects as the table owner, which bypasses RLS unless `FORCE`d). Delivered as an owner-run runbook â€” **deliberately NOT an automated migration**: RLS is raw Postgres DDL outside `schema.prisma`, and a wrong connecting-role assumption could deny every query, so it belongs in the Supabase SQL Editor with a canary step + instant rollback (both included). Per-row tenant policies are scoped as a future step (the app never uses PostgREST today â€” Prisma only). Docs-only. Zielone: `docs:check`.

- **Encrypt NextAuth `Account` OAuth tokens at rest (audit v5)** **(#645)** â€” the stock `@auth/prisma-adapter` stored viewer login-provider `access_token`/`refresh_token`/`id_token` **in cleartext** in the `accounts` table â€” the last plaintext OAuth-token store (the app's own actively-used tokens already live encrypted in `Connection`). The tenant-aware adapter now **encrypts these three fields in `linkAccount`** (before the base insert) and **decrypts them in `getAccount`** (on the way out), so it's transparent to NextAuth while the DB holds only ciphertext. **Back-compat:** `decryptSecret` passes legacy plaintext through unchanged, so pre-#645 rows keep working (and re-encrypt if ever re-linked). Verified the app never reads these DB fields elsewhere (its token reads use the in-memory OAuth callback + the encrypted `Connection` store). **âڑ ï¸ڈ Owner must live-test after deploy** (OAuth sign-in via Google/Discord/Twitch + the YouTube link) â€” WebAuthn-style, can't be exercised locally; passkeys-isolated reasoning doesn't apply here, so confirm sign-in works. No schema change, no db push. Zielone: `tsc`/**473 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **At-rest crypto hardening â€” HKDF key separation + fail-closed PII (audit v5)** **(#644)** â€” two real weaknesses the security pass flagged: (a) the **same** SHA-256-derived key was used for *both* AES-256-GCM encryption **and** HMAC, and (b) `encryptSecret` **failed open** â€” a crypto error silently stored the **plaintext** (dangerous for shipping PII / TOTP secrets). Now: a master key (from `ENCRYPTION_KEY`â€–`NEXTAUTH_SECRET`) feeds **HKDF** to derive **independent** enc + MAC sub-keys, written under a new **`enc:v2:`** envelope; `decryptSecret`/`hmacVerify` still read **`enc:v1:`** (legacy master key) and legacy HMAC sigs, so existing ciphertext + in-flight OAuth `state` keep working and upgrade to v2 on next write â€” **no migration, no db push**. New **`encryptSecretStrict`** (throws instead of leaking plaintext) now guards the two PII writes: `ShippingProfile` (`/api/profile/shipping`) and `User.totpSecret` (`/api/admin/2fa`). `lib/crypto` tests **+5 â†’ 473** (v2 round-trip, v1 back-compat, strict, true key-separation, HMAC v1-fallback). EN+PL n/a (no UI). Zielone: `tsc`/**473 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **PayMedia donations: verified donation-code matching, not spoofable username (audit v4)** **(#637)** â€” the PayMedia webhook credited GT + flipped `isDonator`/`totalDonated` on the account matched by `metadata.username` / `discord_id` â€” fields set on the donation form, i.e. **attacker-controllable**, so a donor could aim GT (and Donator status) at **any** account. This is the same spoofing class the Streamlabs path closed in #612; PayMedia was missed. Now it reuses `matchDonationToUser` and **auto-credits ONLY when the donor's personal code `GE-XXXXXX` is present** in the metadata (message/username/discord fields are scanned for it) â€” codeless donations fall through to the manual admin queue, exactly like Streamlabs. The donation code is globally unique and per-user, so it IS the verification (you can only credit your own account). Idempotency (`externalId` P2002) + currency/amount checks unchanged. Logic-only, no schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

### Fixed

- **Docs refresh + owner runbook (audit v4)** **(#636)** â€” closed the documentation drift the audit found: **ROADMAP** â€” struck the two stale "do zrobienia" items already shipped (`@simplewebauthn` 9â†’13 #629, reactCompilerâ†”eslint #617) and added a fresh "إڑwieإ¼o dowiezione" wave for #618â€“#635; **ENV.md** â€” documented `AUTH_URL` (the Auth.js-v5 alias that takes precedence and that passkeys pin rpID/origin to); **ARCHITECTURE.md آ§9** â€” added the per-tenant game-library models (`Game.tenantId` #618, `GameVote` #628, `GameLibraryConfig.psnNpsso`/`xboxApiKey` #626/#627); **new `docs/OWNER-SETUP.md`** â€” one consolidated checklist for the owner-only actions previously scattered across docs (Game backfill, PSN/Xbox key setup + live test, passkey device test, dedicated prod `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, raffle-bot wiring, infra hygiene). Docs-only. Zielone: `docs:check`.

- **CHANGELOG repair + docs:check gap-detection (audit v4)** **(#633)** â€” restored two entries whose bold titles had been clobbered when later entries were prepended, leaving orphaned bodies with no PR reference: **#629** (`@simplewebauthn` 9â†’13) and **#631** (admin `secDesc_*`). Root cause: `docs:check` only compared the **highest** PR number, so an intermediate gap (e.g. #629 missing while #630 was present) passed green. Hardened `scripts/check-docs-sync.mjs` to verify **every** PR referenced in recent git history appears in the CHANGELOG, not just the max â€” the gap that hid #629 can't recur. Docs/tooling only. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.
- **Game-vote tally was aggregated across all portals in the null-tenant path (audit v4)** **(#632)** â€” on `/games` the "play next" vote tally used `where: { ...(tid ? { tenantId } : {}) }`, so when no tenant resolved (`tid` null) the `where` was **empty** and counted **every portal's** votes globally â€” inconsistent with `myVote`, which correctly scoped to `{ tenantId: null }`. Latent today (single live portal) but a cross-portal leak the moment a second portal exists before subdomain resolution is wired. Now the tally matches `myVote`: `tid ? { tenantId: tid } : { tenantId: null }`. The vote write path (`/api/games/vote`) was already correctly scoped. One-line scoping fix, no schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **Admin section descriptions showed a raw i18n key (audit v4)** **(#631)** â€” 13 admin sections (`recap`, `clipdirector`, `economy`, `payments`, `notifications`, `sponsors`, `collectibles`, `community`, `clanwars`, `trivia`, `twofactor`, `scenes`, `soundrewards`) had no `secDesc_*` translation, so opening e.g. `/admin#payments` literally rendered the string `admin.secDesc_payments` in the help banner. Added all 13 keys (EN + PL) in the friendly explanatory style of the existing ones. UI-only, no code/schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **`@simplewebauthn` 9 â†’ 13 (passkeys, audit v3 hygiene)** **(#629)** â€” bumped `@simplewebauthn/server` + `/browser` four majors to **v13.3.1** and adapted the 4 passkey routes + 2 client calls to the new API: `userID` is now a `Uint8Array`, credential ids are **base64url strings** (not Buffers) in `excludeCredentials`/`verifyAuthenticationResponse`, the verify result moved to `registrationInfo.credential.{id,publicKey,counter}`, the auth verifier takes `credential` (was `authenticator`), the deprecated `@simplewebauthn/types` imports moved to `@simplewebauthn/server`, and the browser `startRegistration`/`startAuthentication` now take `{ optionsJSON }`. **Done before passkeys' first real device test on purpose** â€” there are ~no stored credentials yet, so the upcoming test validates v13 directly (no v9â†’v13 credential-format migration to worry about). Passkeys remain **isolated from OAuth** (a passkey issue can never break OAuth sign-in) and still **need the live device test** before being relied on (unchanged status). `next-auth` keeps a *peerOptional* `@simplewebauthn/server@^9` for its (unused) WebAuthn provider â€” cosmetic warning, verified harmless by a green `build`. tsc verifies the whole adaptation against the installed v13 types. Zielone: `tsc`/**462 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.

- **GDPR data export â€” "download my data" (audit v3)** **(#619)** â€” completes the privacy story we built (encrypted PII #609, erasure, policy #610): a viewer can now **download everything we store about their account** as a JSON file from `/profile` â€” the GDPR **right of access (Art. 15) + portability (Art. 20)** companion to the existing one-click erasure. New **`GET /api/profile/export`** (owner-only, strictly scoped to `session.user.id`, rate-limited 5/5min) gathers the account, economy, progression, social links, GT ledger (capped at 5 000, flagged if trimmed), achievements, collectibles, followed portals, companion, and shipping PII (**decrypted for the owner only**), and streams it as a `Content-Disposition: attachment` file. **Secret material is never exported** â€” the pure `lib/data-export` shaper redacts the TOTP secret, passkey keys and OAuth tokens, emitting only presence (`totpEnabled`, `passkeys: N`); internal moderation notes and other people's data are excluded by design. A small self-contained `DataExportCard` on `/profile` (fetch â†’ client-side download). Pure `lib/data-export` (`buildUserExport` redaction + `exportFilename` slug, **+8 tests â†’ 439**). - **Per-portal game library (audit v3, white-label)** **(#618)** â€” the game library (`/games`, synced from Steam/PSN) was the **last globally-keyed feature**: `Game` had a global `@@unique([source, externalId])`, so two portals couldn't each own the same Steam appid and every portal saw the founder's library. Now `Game` gains a nullable **`tenantId`** and the unique becomes the per-tenant composite **`@@unique([tenantId, source, externalId])`** (+`@@index([tenantId])`) â€” **db push** (the unique swap needs `--accept-data-loss`; no real loss â€” the column is all-NULL and rows stay unique under the new key). The Steam/PSN sync now writes `tenantId` (from the per-tenant `GameLibraryConfig`), **bulk-claims any legacy NULL-tenant rows for the portal before upserting** (so a re-sync updates them in place instead of creating duplicates â€” robust regardless of backfill order), prunes only the portal's own rows, and uses a NULL-safe upsert helper (Prisma can't key an upsert on a compound unique with a NULL member). All reads are scoped **OR-null** (`/api/games`, `/games`, `/admin#games` count/aggregate/list) and `toggle_hidden` is tenant-guarded (`updateMany` by id+tenant â†’ can't flip another portal's game). Existing rows are attached to the founder by **`/api/admin/backfill-tenant`** (now also backfills `Game`). **Per-tenant PSN/Xbox *connect* (sensitive NPSSO per portal) remains a subdomain-milestone follow-up** â€” the NPSSO is still a single global env. Founder portal unchanged (its rows claim/backfill to its tenant). Zielone: `tsc`/**431 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.

Hooked into the existing `/api/support/click` beacon, **throttled to one alert per method per 5 min** (a click is an intent signal, not a confirmed payment â€” fail-closed so a limiter blip can't spam) and fully best-effort (never blocks the beacon). - **Chat-keyword raffle with sub/mod odds (audit v3)** **(#611)** â€” the classic "type a word in chat to enter, streamer draws later" giveaway. - **Encrypted shipping/contact profile for physical rewards (audit v3)** **(#609)** â€” viewers can now store the shipping details needed to send them a **physical prize** (full name, phone, email, address, city, postal code, country, **parcel locker** e.g. InPost). New **`ShippingProfile`** model (**db push** â€” new table, applied) kept deliberately **out of the heavily-`select`ed `users` table** so it can never be swept into a select-less query and can be dropped independently. **Every sensitive field is encrypted at rest** (AES-256-GCM via `lib/crypto`, `enc:v1:` envelope); only `country` (ISO-2) is plaintext. `GET/PUT/DELETE /api/profile/shipping` is strictly scoped to `session.user.id` (owner-only, rate-limited): **PUT requires an explicit consent checkbox** (GDPR Art. 6/7, stamps `consentAt`) and re-encrypts; **DELETE is one-click GDPR erasure**. - **P2P GT gifting** **(#553)** â€” direction 2: viewers can **send %gt% to each other**. A "Send %gt%" button on a viewer's public profile (`/u/<name>`, for logged-in non-owners) â†’ amount â†’ `POST /api/gift`. The debit + credit + both ledger rows are **one atomic transaction** (`gte` guard â†’ no overspend); anti-abuse: **can't gift yourself**, **5 000 per-transfer + 10 000 rolling-24h caps**, per-IP rate-limited, recipient resolved **within the same portal**. The recipient gets a best-effort in-app **notification** (created outside the tx so it can never undo a real transfer). No new model (existing `Transaction`/`Notification`). Pure `lib/gift` (`clampGift`/`giftError`, **+5 tests**). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**383 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **P2P card marketplace** **(#552)** â€” marketplace phase 2: viewers **trade collectible cards (#551) for %gt%** on `/market`. List a card you own (it's **escrowed** â€” removed from your collection while listed), browse others' listings and **buy**, or cancel to get the card back. Every GT + card move is **one atomic transaction** with `gte`/`qty` guards: the listing is claimed with a conditional `UPDATE` (so two concurrent buys yield exactly one sale), overspend is impossible, you can't buy your own listing, and a failed payment rolls the whole thing back. A **5% fee is burned** on each sale (a GT sink, reviewed for value-conservation). Model `CardListing` (**db push** â€” new table, per-tenant). Pure `lib/market` (price clamp + fee, **+3 tests**); buy/sell/my-listings UI. In the Community nav + Ctrl/âŒک K. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**378 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Collectible cards + GT packs** **(#551)** â€” marketplace phase 1: the **tradeable asset** the P2P market (#552) will sit on. A per-portal card catalog (`/admin#collectibles` â€” name, **rarity**, emoji/image) that viewers collect on `/collectibles` by **opening GT packs** â€” one card per pack, **weighted by rarity** (common 60 / rare 28 / epic 10 / legendary 2). The GT spend + ownership grant + ledger entry are **one atomic transaction** (`tokens: { gte }` guard â†’ overspend-proof). Models `Collectible` + `UserCollectible` (**db push** â€” new tables, per-tenant). Pure `lib/collectibles` (`pickRarity`/weights, **+5 tests**). Collection grid shows owned cards in full colour (أ—qty) and the rest as dimmed silhouettes. In the Community nav + Ctrl/âŒک K. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**375 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.

- **Passkeys â€” passwordless sign-in (stage 2)** **(#544)** â€” a **"Sign in with a passkey"** button on the sign-in page completes the feature: a usernameless/discoverable WebAuthn assertion is verified server-side, and on success a **session is minted directly** â€” a `Session` row + the host-only `authjs.session-token` cookie, an **exact replication of NextAuth's database-session sign-in** (cookie name/attrs/value verified against `@auth/core`). **It never reads or alters the NextAuth config or the OAuth providers** â€” it only ADDS a session for that browser, so the worst possible failure is "didn't sign in," never "broke OAuth login." Routes `/api/auth/passkey/login/{options,verify}`; the signature counter advances on each use (clone detection). No schema change. **Needs a real-device test on the live site** (WebAuthn needs HTTPS + an authenticator â€” can't be exercised locally). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**341 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Passkeys â€” registration & management (stage 1)** **(#543)** â€” viewers can add **passkeys** (fingerprint / face / device PIN) to their account from a self-hiding "Passkeys" card on `/profile`: a full WebAuthn registration ceremony (`/api/auth/passkey/register/options` â†’ `â€¦/verify`, challenge stashed in a short-lived httpOnly cookie) backed by `@simplewebauthn/server`, plus list/remove (`/api/auth/passkey`). **Deliberately additive and isolated â€” touches ZERO of the existing OAuth login flow**; the model `Passkey` (per-user, `credentialId @unique`, **db push** â€” new table) just stores credentials. Pure `lib/webauthn` host/origin helpers (**+5 tests**). New deps `@simplewebauthn/server`+`browser`. **Signing IN with a passkey is the next stage (#544)** â€” it'll mint a `Session` row directly (DB-session strategy), still without altering the NextAuth config. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**341 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Fixed

- **next-intl `INVALID_KEY` noise from dotted message keys** **(#597)** â€” every page render logged ~30أ— `INVALID_KEY: Namespace keys cannot contain the character "."` (thrown from `getTranslations` in the locale layout + `page` `generateMetadata`) because eight Twitch/Kick event-type labels were keyed by their **literal dotted event names** (`admin.twitchEventSub.eventType."channel.subscribe"`, `admin.kickEvents.eventLabel."livestream.status.updated"`, â€¦), which next-intl reads as nesting separators â€” so those keys never resolved (silent EN fallback) and the log was pure noise. Renamed all eight to a safe **underscore** separator (`channel_subscribe`, `livestream_status_updated`, â€¦) across **all 14 locale catalogs** (key parity intact, EN stays the deep-merge base), matching the existing underscore convention already used in `webhooksOut.eventLabel`; the two consumers (`TwitchEventSub`/`KickEvents`) now normalize the dotted raw event type (`type.replace(/\./g, "_")`) before the `t.raw(...)` label lookup, so labels still render. Data + 2 components only, no schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Security

- **Verified-only donation crediting via a personal code (audit v3)** **(#612)** â€” closes the within-tenant half of the Streamlabs spoofing finding (#601 fixed cross-tenant). The old auto-match credited GT by the **donor-supplied name / `@mention`**, so a payer could aim a donation's GT at **any account**. Removed entirely: `matchDonationToUser` now auto-credits **only** when the donation message contains the donor's **personal code** (`GE-XXXXXX`, shown on their profile, lazily minted, globally unique) â€” resolved tenant-scoped; everything else falls to the **manual admin queue** (`/api/admin/donations`, unchanged). New `User.donationCode` (**db push** â€” additive nullable unique column, applied with `--accept-data-loss` for the new-column unique, owner-approved; no real data loss â€” all rows null). New `GET /api/profile/donation-code` (owner-only, lazy-mint w/ collision retry) + a **`DonationCodeCard`** on `/profile` (code + copy + how-to). Pure `lib/donation-code` (`generate`/`extract`/`isValid`, **+5 tests â†’ 431**). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**431 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Security hardening sweep â€” TOTP / passkey / webhook / CSRF + donation GT cap (audit v3)** **(#602)** â€” five low/medium findings from the v3 audit, all no-schema: (1) **TOTP step-up** compared the 6-digit code with `===` â†’ now a **constant-time** `timingSafeEqual` so a near-miss can't be probed digit-by-digit (RFC test vectors still green). (2) **Passkey login** wrote back the signature counter but never rejected a **non-advancing counter** (the classic cloned-authenticator signal) â†’ now refuses the login when `newCounter !== 0 && newCounter <= stored`. (3) **Outbound webhooks** ran the SSRF guard on the original URL but `fetch` followed redirects â†’ added **`redirect:"manual"`** so an admin-set public URL can't 302 into `169.254.169.254`/internal (a 3xx is counted as a failure). (4) **Streamlabs OAuth callback** skipped the CSRF-nonce check when the cookie was absent â†’ now **requires** the cookie AND a match. (5) **Streamlabs donation GT** minted `amount أ— GT_PER_PLN` **ignoring currency** and uncapped â†’ now **currency-converted** via `plnFromCurrency` and **capped** at ~100k-PLN-equivalent so a non-PLN or malformed-huge upstream amount can't over-mint. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**418 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Scope donation / sub / cheer crediting to the event's portal (audit v3)** **(#601)** â€” a fresh deep audit found the GT-crediting lookups for **Streamlabs donations** and **Twitch/Kick subآ·giftآ·cheer** events resolved the credited user by **username globally, with no tenant filter** â€” so a real (signed/verified) event on portal A whose donor-name/Twitch-login also exists on portal B would **mint GT into portal B's economy** (a cross-tenant economic leak; also the donor-supplied name/`@mention` in Streamlabs let a payer aim the credit at any same-named account). All six webhook credit lookups (`twitch-eventsub` sub/gift/cheer, `kick-events` sub/gift/cheer) now scope the `Connection` match by **`user.tenantId`**, and `matchDonationToUser` (Streamlabs) scopes by **`User.tenantId`** threaded from the connection â€” both using the established **`OR: [{tenantId}, {tenantId: null}]`** back-compat pattern, so single-tenant (null tenant) behaviour is byte-for-byte unchanged and only multi-tenant crediting gets isolated. No schema change, no db push. (Deferred to a follow-up: the within-tenant donor-name spoofing hardening â€” needs an owner call on disabling name/mention auto-match â€” plus Streamlabs currency-aware GT cap and the LOW hardenings: TOTP constant-time compare, passkey clone-counter rejection, outbound-webhook `redirect:"manual"`.) Zielone: `tsc`/**418 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Cross-tenant scoping for stream/donation/moderation data + per-tenant bot secret (Batch B, audit v2)** **(#599)** â€” the last audit-v2 gap: four bot/webhook-fed models had **no `tenantId`**, so their data was a single global pool â€” latent at single-tenant, but a cross-tenant leak the moment subdomains light up. Added a **nullable `tenantId`** (+ index) to **`StreamSession`**, **`Donation`** and **`ModViolationLog`** and a nullable **`Tenant.botSecret`** (**db push** â€” all additive, no `--accept-data-loss`). Writes now tag the resolved portal: stream-session create/close carry the EventSub-resolved tenant (and one portal's `stream.offline` can no longer close another's live session), Streamlabs/YouTube donations use the connection's `tenantId`, mod-violation logs use `currentTenantId()`. Admin reads scope to the caller's tenant (`/api/admin/analytics` sessions, `/api/admin/mod-violations` stats, `/api/admin/section-data` unmatched donations) and the manual donation-match (`/api/admin/donations`) refuses another portal's donation. New **`verifyBotSecretForTenant`** (+6 tests) accepts a tenant's own `botSecret` **or** the global `BOT_SECRET` as fallback. **Fully backward-compatible / latent**: at single-tenant `currentTenantId()` is null â†’ writes tag null, reads stay unscoped â†’ identical behaviour; the global bot secret keeps working. **Deferred within this batch:** scoping the `ChatActivityBucket` heatmap (needs a destructive composite-PK change â€” done at subdomain-enable) and *enforcing* per-tenant bot secrets (needs each tenant running its own bot, coordinated with the `ghost-empire-chat` repo). Zielone: `tsc`/**418 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Atomic gift daily-cap + account-XP under concurrency (audit v2)** **(#573)** â€” two read-modify-write races, both fixed with a `SELECT â€¦ FOR UPDATE` row lock on the affected user: (1) **Gift daily cap** â€” the rolling-24h `GIFT_DAILY_LIMIT` was checked *before* the transfer transaction, so a burst of concurrent gifts each passed the stale pre-check and committed, **defeating the anti-laundering cap** (balance was still safe via the `gte` guard); the cap is now **re-asserted inside the locked transaction**. (2) **Account XP** â€” `awardAccountXp` read `xp`, added, then wrote the **absolute** value, so concurrent awards on the hot chat-award path clobbered each other (ended at `X+max(a,b)`, not `X+a+b`); now the readâ†’computeâ†’write runs under the row lock (level/prestige/bonus derived from the locked value), with the alert + achievement side-effects moved **after commit**. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Scope admin reads to the resolved tenant (audit v2)** **(#572)** â€” four admin reads ignored the host tenant and hit a global/legacy row, leaking or mis-showing another portal's data: **`/api/admin/alerts`** listed recent alerts with **no `where`** (exposed other tenants' alert actor names + donation/sub amounts) â†’ now scoped to `{ tenantId }` (+ legacy null); **`/api/admin/section-data?s=bot`** read/created the legacy `id:"default"` `BotConfig` â†’ now the tenant's row (mirrors `admin/bot-config`), so a tenant admin no longer sees/edits the founder's reward rates; **`/api/admin/stream-goals`** read the `id:"default"` `HypeTrainState` â†’ now per-tenant (mirrors overlay-feeds); **`/api/admin/setup-status`** read `moderationConfig.findFirst()` (an arbitrary portal's row) â†’ now scoped. All three models already have `tenantId @unique`; only these reads were unscoped. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Rate-limit the un-capped cost/abuse endpoints (audit v2)** **(#571)** â€” three endpoints could run up cost or fan-out unbounded: **`POST /api/admin/recap`** made a real LLM call (+ optional Discord post) with **no limiter** (every other AI route self-limits) â†’ now **10/5min per admin**; **`POST /api/push/test`** fanned out to the user's devices + the external push provider on every call â†’ now **5/min per user**; **`POST /api/bot/ai-reply`** was limited only by the **attacker-controllable** `username` key â†’ added a **global cap (300/h)** so rotating usernames can't multiply AI spend (mirrors `bot/imagine`). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Resolver atomicity + admin step-up (audit v2)** **(#569)** â€” four correctness/authz gaps from the second audit: (1) **Heist double-resolve** â€” `resolveHeist` did a plain read + unconditional `update`, so the bot timer racing the lazy recovery-on-join could both run the payout loop and **double-credit the crew**; now it **atomically claims** the heist (`updateMany openâ†’resolving`, bail on `count===0`) like predictions/duels. (2) **weekly-rewards cron paid a single GLOBAL top-3** (`getCachedWeeklyRanking(null)`) while the ranking pages are per-tenant, and its idempotency was a global check-then-act; now it **loops every portal**, pays each its own top-3, and guards with a **per-tenant-per-week unique `externalId`** (a double cron-fire loses with P2002, atomically). (3) **Role grants lacked step-up** â€” `admin`/`moderator` changes (the most powerful, role-conferring actions) were weaker than a reversible `ban-user`; now they **require a fresh 2FA code** (`requireStepUp`, no-op without 2FA; client uses `apiPostStepUp`). (4) **Admin token deduction** wasn't atomic (stale pre-check + unguarded `increment`); now a `gte`-guarded `updateMany` so concurrent deducts can't drive a balance negative. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Casino concurrency hardening â€” per-session lock on stateful games (audit v2)** **(#568)** â€” a second deep audit found the stateful Redis games did **non-atomic read-modify-write** with no lock: in Mines `reveal` / Hi-Lo `guess`, two concurrent moves could interleave so a winning-tile `set` lands *after* a losing-tile `del`, **resurrecting a session that should have ended** (erasing the loss â†’ GT over-payout); Blackjack `double` also charged a second bet *before* claiming the session (concurrent doubles â†’ an extra debit with no game). New **`withLock`** in `lib/redis` (Redis `SET NX PX` + atomic Lua compare-and-delete release, auto-expiring) now serializes every in-place session mutation â€” Mines `reveal`, Hi-Lo `guess`, Blackjack `hit`/`stand`/`double` â€” so concurrent moves on one session can't interleave (the loser gets a 409 "retry"). Cash-out/settle were already atomic via `GETDEL`; this closes the intermediate race. Fail-open if Redis blips (the `GETDEL` claims still protect payouts). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Clear all `npm audit` alerts via overrides (no breaking downgrades)** **(#567)** â€” the 5 moderate advisories were all **transitive dev/build** deps: `postcss <8.5.10` (CSS-stringify XSS, GHSA-qx2v-qp2m-jg93) pinned by **`next`**, and `@hono/node-server <1.19.13` (serveStatic middleware bypass, GHSA-92pp-h63x-v22m) pulled by **`@prisma/dev`** (Prisma 7 tooling). `npm audit fix --force` wanted to downgrade `next`â†’9 / `prisma`â†’6 â€” rejected. Instead added npm **`overrides`**: `postcss ^8.5.10` scoped under `next` (so it dedupes to the already-installed 8.5.15) and `@hono/node-server ^1.19.13`. Lockfile regenerated to apply them; **verified no runtime dep changed** (next/react/prisma/next-auth/next-intl/stripe/zod all identical) and the **Vercel Linux native binaries** (`@next/swc-linux-*`, `lightningcss-linux-x64-gnu`, `@tailwindcss/oxide-linux-x64-gnu`, `@img/sharp-linux-x64`) are intact. **`npm audit` now: 0 vulnerabilities.** No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build` + `npm audit` clean.
- **Audit follow-up â€” medium-severity fixes (M1/M2/M3/M4)** **(#556)** â€” second pass from the same audit, all multi-tenant / concurrency correctness:
  - **M1 â€” overlay token cross-tenant leak:** `isValidOverlayToken` (`lib/alerts`) accepted the legacy "default" row's token AND the global `OVERLAY_TOKEN` env var for **any** tenant â€” so one portal's (or the env) token could drive another portal's OBS overlay. Now **strict 1:1**: a real tenant validates only against its own `overlayToken`; the default-row + env fallback survive only for the legacy/founder portal (`tid === null`, the owner's own).
  - **M2 â€” merge-users null-tenant bypass:** the tenant-isolation guard only ran `if (tid)` and used `u.tenantId && u.tenantId !== tid`, so a per-tenant admin could merge (and thereby delete) a **null-tenant** (legacy/global) user. Now strict equality (`u.tenantId !== tid`), **always enforced** for non-platform-owners â€” both users must belong to exactly the acting admin's portal.
  - **M3 â€” predictions TOCTOU:** `resolvePrediction` snapshotted entries + pot, then claimed the row â€” a wager committing in between left a paid-for stake unpaid. Wager / resolve / cancel now take a **`SELECT â€¦ FOR UPDATE`** row lock on the prediction up front, serializing all three on that row.
  - **M4 â€” daily-bonus double-claim:** replaced the Serializable-isolation + in-tx re-check with a **deterministic unique `externalId`** (`daily-bonus:<userId>:<utcDay>`) on the already-unique `Transaction.externalId` â€” two concurrent claims race on the unique index and exactly one wins (P2002). (The drops "first-N bonus" atomic counter, also M4, rides the batched perf-index **db push** in a later PR.)
  No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Security hardening from a full audit (C1/H1/H2/H3)** **(#555)** â€” fixes four access-control / SSRF gaps found in an adversarial pass over the admin + outbound-fetch surface:
  - **C1 â€” destructive admin reset was per-tenant-admin reachable:** `POST /api/admin/reset-database` runs **global** `deleteMany`s that span EVERY tenant, but was gated by `requireAdmin` (any portal admin). Now gated by **`requirePlatformOwner`** + a **fresh-2FA step-up** (`requireStepUp` â€” the single most destructive action in the app), with the danger-zone UI retrying via `apiPostStepUp`.
  - **H1 â€” cross-tenant data export:** `GET /api/admin/backup` reads every user's GT balance + role flags across **all** tenants (empty `where`), also only `requireAdmin`. Now **`requirePlatformOwner`**.
  - **H2 â€” unauthenticated IDOR on link analytics:** `POST /api/profile/social-click` did `update({ where: { id } })` from a raw client id â€” any id could bump (or cross-tenant forge) another user's click counter. Now an **`updateMany` scoped to a link whose owner is in the current portal** (mirrors the support/click route).
  - **H3 â€” SSRF via admin webhooks:** outgoing webhooks (`lib/webhooks-out`) `fetch`ed admin-set URLs with no destination check. New **`lib/ssrf-guard`** (`isSafeWebhookUrl` â€” rejects loopback/private/link-local/CGNAT/cloud-metadata both as IP literals AND after DNS resolution; `http(s)` only) is now enforced before every delivery and surfaced on the test button (**+ unit tests**).
  - Also unblocks the type gate: `scripts/seed-collectibles.ts` was a global script colliding with `seed-achievements.ts` on top-level `main` (TS2393) â€” marked it a module with `export {};` (the `backfill-account-tenant.ts` pattern). This was making a fresh `tsc` (CI) red.
  No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Hardening pass from an adversarial review of the new auth + push code** **(#545)** â€” two self-reviews of the just-shipped passkey (#543/#544) and web-push (#533â€“#535) code surfaced fixable gaps (no auth-bypass; the core crypto + tenant isolation were already correct):
  - **Passkeys:** `rpID`/`origin` **and** the minted session cookie's name/`secure` are now pinned to the canonical `AUTH_URL`/`NEXTAUTH_URL` instead of the spoofable `Host`/`X-Forwarded-Proto` headers (kills host-header trust + guarantees the cookie matches what NextAuth reads); the WebAuthn **challenge is strictly single-use** (cookie cleared on every terminal path, not just success); login now **requires user verification** (biometric/PIN â€” appropriate for a sole login factor); the login endpoints are **rate-limited** and no longer leak a **credential-existence oracle** (generic `not-verified` for unknown-vs-failed); client-supplied `transports` are whitelisted. (+4 tests.)
  - **Web push:** the "LIVE now" push is now **fire-and-forget** in the Twitch EventSub webhook (was `await`ed â€” a slow push endpoint could have stalled the webhook â†’ Twitch retries / DB-pool exhaustion), and every `web-push` send now carries a **5s timeout** so a black-holed endpoint can't hang the function; defensive `.catch` on all fire-and-forget `notify*` call sites.
  No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**345 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Performance

- **Aggregate poll/prediction tallies in the DB instead of loading every row (audit v3)** **(#606)** â€” two read-hot paths pulled whole child tables to count in JS. **`POST /api/polls/vote`** re-read **every `PollVote` row** of the poll on each vote (`findMany` + `.filter().length` per option) â†’ now one **`groupBy`** (the table already has `@@index([pollId, optionIndex])`), matching the pattern the overlay feed already uses. **`GET /api/predictions`** (public, `force-dynamic`) loaded **all `PredictionEntry` rows of every open prediction** on each request to compute per-option totals â†’ now a single **`groupBy(["predictionId","optionIndex"])`** across all active predictions plus **one scoped `findMany`** for the caller's own entries (`myEntry`). A hyped poll/prediction with thousands of entries no longer streams them all per request â€” big win on the 3-connection pool. (P3 â€” batching the per-loser `notification.create` in prediction resolve/cancel â€” left as low-value/money-path-adjacent.) No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**418 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Atomic + batched stream-goal increments; batched daily-quest progress (audit v2)** **(#600)** â€” a fresh-eyes pass on the event hot paths found two per-row write loops. **`incrementGoals`** (fires on every sub / gift-sub / follow / donation / cheer / YT-member) read each active goal, computed `current + amount` in JS, then wrote the **absolute** value back per goal in a loop â€” a **read-modify-write lost-update race** (two concurrent monetary events both read `current`, both wrote the sum â†’ one bump silently lost, goal bars undercount), the same class as the account-XP fix (#573), plus an N-query loop. Now it's **one atomic `updateMany({ current: { increment } })`** for all matching goals (no lost updates under concurrency) + a single guarded `updateMany` to stamp `completedAt` on goals that crossed their target â€” **2 queries, race-free**, in a `$transaction`. **`updateDailyTaskProgress`** (fires on every awarded chat/Discord message) issued **N sequential `upsert`s** (one per active quest of that type) on the 3-connection pool â†’ now one **`$transaction`** of the same upserts (one round-trip; each upsert keeps its atomic create-or-increment, so semantics are unchanged). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**418 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Perf tail â€” OG cache + parallel entry reads (audit v2)** **(#576)** â€” the profile **OG image** (`/u/<name>` opengraph-image) had no `revalidate`, so every social-scrape re-ran a Prisma read + Satori PNG render â†’ added `revalidate = 600` (10 min). `/api/clips` and `/api/collectibles` awaited `auth()` then `currentTenantId()` **serially** â†’ now `Promise.all([...])` so the two independent reads don't stack a round-trip on the 3-connection pool. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Cache the public `/support` page + casino leaderboard (audit v2)** **(#575)** â€” both were fully uncached public reads. `/support` ran **5 DB queries** (incl. a `groupBy` for top supporters) **plus CPU-bound per-method QR generation** on every visit â†’ the whole shaped blob is now `cacheJson`-cached per tenant (**60s**), and the page-QR per host (**5min**). `GET /api/gt-games/leaderboard` ran a **30-day `groupBy`** over the high-volume casino table per request â†’ now cached per tenant (**60s**, mirrors `getCachedRanking`). Big drop in DB/CPU work on two hot public paths (3-connection pool). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Chat-award hot path â€” ack-first, secondary effects in background (audit v2)** **(#574)** â€” `/api/internal/chat-award` fires **once per chat message across Twitch/Kick/YouTube** (the single hottest write path) and ran, strictly serially after the GT award, three more best-effort effects â€” battle-pass XP (`awardSeasonXp`), daily-quest progress (`updateDailyTaskProgress`) and the activity-heatmap upsert â€” ~6 extra serial round-trips on a **3-connection** pool. The bot only needs `awarded`/`newBalance`, so those three now run in **`after()`** (post-response, `waitUntil`); the bot's per-message call returns right after the award transaction. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Timeouts on all third-party API calls (audit v2)** **(#570)** â€” outbound calls to **Twitch / Kick / YouTube / Streamlabs / Steam** had **no timeout**, so a slow/black-holed upstream could hang a serverless function and **pin one of the 3 DB-pool slots** indefinitely (e.g. `helixGet` backs the live-status banner; Kick `getPublicKey` is on the webhook signature-verification path). New **`lib/http.httpFetch`** wraps `fetch` with a default **8s `AbortSignal.timeout`** (override via your own `signal`); every external `fetch` in those five clients now goes through it, so a stuck upstream **fails fast** instead of hanging (callers already handle the rejection). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Per-tenant composite indexes + atomic drop-bonus counter** **(#561)** â€” one batched **db push** (additive, no data loss). Six composite indexes for hot tenant-scoped reads that the existing single-column indexes didn't cover: `Companion[tenantId,xp]` (companion leaderboard), `Clan[tenantId,treasury]` + `Clan[tenantId,warPoints]` (clan + clan-war rankings), `StreamGoal[tenantId,active]` (active-goals reads on the overlay/incrementGoals path), `StreamAlert[tenantId,type,createdAt]` (recent/top-supporters & type-filtered alert reads), `UserCollectible[userId,acquiredAt]` (owned-cards newest-first). Also closes the deferred **#audit-M4 drops** finding: the "first N claimers get the bonus" check was an out-of-transaction `count()` (N racers could all read 0 and all grab the bonus â†’ over-minted GT); it's now an **atomic `StreamDrop.claimCount` ordinal** incremented inside the claim transaction (row-locked, so exactly the first `bonusSlots` win). **db push** (additive: 6 indexes + `claimCount Int @default(0)`). Zielone: `tsc`/**392 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **`/market` â€” bound the unbounded reads** **(#560)** â€” the marketplace GET capped active listings (`take: 60`) but loaded the viewer's whole owned-card collection and own listings with no `take`. Added `take: 200` to the owned-card picker (it's the trade selector, not the full collection page â€” generous bound vs. a payload that grows with the catalog) and `take: MAX_ACTIVE_LISTINGS` to the own-listings read (already business-bounded, now defensively too). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Semantic search â€” shared (Redis) embeddings + in-flight dedup** **(#559)** â€” the `/search` embeddings (#554) lived in **per-instance `Map`s**, so every cold serverless instance re-embedded the whole corpus, and concurrent first-hits on one instance each fired their own OpenAI batch. Both now go through the shared **`cacheJson`** (Upstash Redis â†’ **cross-instance**; per-instance memory fallback when Redis is off): the corpus key carries a content hash (an edited page/achievement/shop item rolls to a fresh key â†’ auto re-embed), with TTLs of **6h** (corpus) / **1h** (query). An **in-flight dedup** map coalesces concurrent identical embeds on one instance so a cold start under load fires **one** batch, not N. Dormant/failed embeds throw a sentinel so they're never cached. Fewer OpenAI calls (cost + latency); pure `lib/semantic` unchanged. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Twitch EventSub webhook â€” ack-first, process in background** **(#558)** â€” the webhook ran every grant handler + the achievement/season-XP fan-out **synchronously before replying**, so a busy stream (hype-train progress storms, gift-sub bursts) on a **3-connection** DB pool could push the response past Twitch's timeout â†’ retries and eventually a **disabled subscription**. Now everything that gates correctness â€” signature + freshness verification and the **idempotency insert** (a retry still loses with P2002) â€” stays synchronous, the tenant is resolved (needs request scope), and then the slow grant/notify/achievement work runs in **`after()`** (Next 16; the platform keeps the function alive via `waitUntil`). Twitch gets a fast 2xx; the background work still completes. Retry/partial-processing semantics are unchanged (handler errors were already swallowed + 200'd). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Overlay hot-path caching â€” ~3 fewer DB queries per poll** **(#557)** â€” the OBS overlay SSE feed runs ~1أ—/s **per browser source**, and each tick read alert settings + per-type configs + validated the overlay token = ~3â€“4 DB round-trips on a connection pool capped at **3**. Those three reads change only on admin edits, so they now go through the shared **`cacheJson`** (Upstash Redis, cross-instance; in-memory fallback when Redis is off) with short TTLs (settings/type-configs **10s**, token list **30s**). `isValidOverlayToken` caches the token *list* (the constant-time compare stays uncached, so a caller can't poison the cache); `getSettings`/`getAlertTypeConfigs` gained an opt-in `{ cached: true }` used **only** on the overlay hot path â€” admin reads/writes stay live. Token rotation **busts** the cache immediately (new `cacheDelete`) so a re-pasted OBS URL works at once. Per poll the feed drops from ~4 queries to ~1 (the live alert fetch). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Code Quality

- **Resolve the React-Compiler â†” ESLint contradiction (audit v3 hygiene)** **(#617)** â€” `next.config` has **`reactCompiler: true`** (the compiler is live), but `eslint.config.mjs` disabled its four correctness rules with a comment claiming *"we don't use the React Compiler"* â€” a misleading config the v3 stack audit flagged as its one genuinely risky spot. Measured the real fallout (turned the rules on: **101 warnings** â€” ~88 `set-state-in-effect` from idiomatic data-fetch effects, plus a few `purity`/`refs` in live-countdown overlays). The compiler **bails out** of optimizing such components rather than miscompiling them, so the app is correct; the rules stay **off** (turning them on + refactoring 101 spots is a separate deliberate sweep, not a build gate) but the **comment is now truthful** about why. No behaviour/schema change. (Routine patch/minor dep bumps intentionally deferred â€” 0 prod vulns, current stack, lockfile/linux-binary risk outweighs marginal gain; the only meaningful version work is `@simplewebauthn` 9â†’13, a careful upgrade for the passkey device-test milestone.) Zielone: `tsc`/**431 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Shared `useToast` provider â€” one toast system instead of nine (audit v2)** **(#598)** â€” nine components each re-implemented the same floating-toast feedback (`useState<{kind,msg}>` + a manual `setTimeout` dismissal + a copy-pasted `fixed bottom-6 end-6 â€¦ shadow-2xl` div with a Check/X icon), with subtly different dismiss timings and **inconsistent or missing `role`/`aria-live`**. New **`lib/`-less `components/ToastProvider`** (mounted once in `Providers`) exposes a `useToast()` hook (`show(kind,msg)` / `ok` / `err`) and renders a single accessible toast stack: correct `role="status"`/`"alert"` + `aria-live` per kind, click-to-dismiss, FIFO-capped at 3, consistent auto-dismiss. Migrated **Shop آ· Admin آ· Predictions آ· Polls آ· Events آ· Seasons آ· Quests آ· Market آ· Collectibles** to it, deleting their local toast state/timers/markup (Admin's OAuth-callback toasts and the per-section `onToast` callback keep working unchanged). Intentionally left the **inline, in-flow** feedback (Clips/Clans/Companion/Portals/Referral/Sounds/Trivia banners + the tiny accent/country/gift/passkey error spans) as-is â€” those render in context by design, not as floating toasts. Net âˆ’~120 lines of duplication; messages stay caller-localized so the provider is i18n-agnostic. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Accessibility

- **Enlarge cramped icon-button tap targets (audit v2)** **(#596)** â€” several icon-only buttons were below a comfortable touch size, especially awkward on mobile. The **viewer-facing** ones are now **â‰¥40أ—40px**: the `/profile` social-link save/remove buttons, the `/market` "my listings" cancel button, and the `/support` reveal/copy/QR action buttons (all via `min-w/min-h` or `w-10 h-10` + flex-centering â€” **icon glyphs unchanged**, only the hit area grows). The dense `/admin#goals` row (enable/reset/delete) went 24pxâ†’**36px** â€” a real bump without bloating the admin list. Every enlarged icon button also gained an `aria-label`. Verified the exact rendered dimensions against the live CSS bundle (40/40/36px) and confirmed no row-layout regression. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Escape closes the header dropdowns (audit v2)** **(#591)** â€” the theme picker, notification bell and account menu closed on outside-click but not on **Escape**, so keyboard users couldn't dismiss them. Added an Esc-to-close listener to all three (theme + bell extend their existing outside-click effect; the account menu, which used a click backdrop, gets a keydown effect). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Bound numeric admin inputs (audit v2)** **(#590)** â€” the shared `FieldInput` accepted `type` but never forwarded `min`/`max`/`step`, so every numeric admin field was unconstrained in-browser. Added the forwarding and applied sensible bounds to the clear-cut fields: drop reward/bonus/slots `min=0`, expiry `min=1`; schedule hour `0â€“23`, minute `0â€“59`, duration `min=1`. Server-side validation is unchanged â€” this just constrains input at the source. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Make the shop-confirm & ranking-admin modals real dialogs (audit v2)** **(#586)** â€” the `/shop` purchase-confirm modal (which spends currency) and the ranking player-admin modal were full-screen overlays with **no `role="dialog"`, no `aria-modal`, no focus management** â€” invisible to screen readers as modals and Tab-leaky. Both now declare `role="dialog"` + `aria-modal="true"` + an `aria-label` (the item / player name) and use the shared **`useFocusTrap`** (focus in, trap Tab, Esc closes when idle, restore focus on close). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Focus-trap the admin editor dialogs (audit v2)** **(#585)** â€” the achievement / event / shop-item editor modals declared `role="dialog" aria-modal="true"` but didn't actually trap focus, so keyboard users could Tab into the obscured page behind and there was no Escape-to-close or focus restore (the `aria-modal` was a lie to screen readers). All three now use the shared **`useFocusTrap`** (focus the dialog on open, trap Tab, **Esc closes** when not busy, restore focus to the trigger on close) and their **X close buttons gained an `aria-label`**. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Announce admin feedback + make clickable rows real controls (audit v2)** **(#579)** â€” three quick a11y wins: the **admin toast** (`AdminClient`) â€” the primary save/create/delete feedback for the whole panel â€” was a silent `<div>`; it now carries `role="status"`/`aria-live="polite"` (errors `role="alert"`/`assertive`), so screen-reader users hear every outcome. **NotificationItem** (`NotificationBell`) was a clickable `<div>` (unreachable by keyboard for link-less notifications) â†’ now a real `<Link>`/`<button>`. **MergeUsers** selection card was a clickable `<div>` â†’ now `role="button"` + `tabIndex` + `aria-pressed` + Enter/Space handler. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Reusable focus trap + ARIA for the command palette / gift popover / accent picker** **(#564)** â€” the codebase had **no focus-management utility**, so overlays only half-managed focus (focus the input, maybe) and never restored it. New **`lib/use-focus-trap`** hook does the three things a11y needs: on open it moves focus inside (caller's `initialFocus`, else first focusable), while open it **traps Tab/Shift+Tab** inside the container and fires `onEscape`, and on close it **restores focus to the trigger**. Applied to: **CommandPalette** (#548) â€” now a proper combobox/listbox (`role="combobox"` + `aria-expanded`/`aria-controls`/`aria-activedescendant`/`aria-autocomplete` on the input; `role="listbox"` on the results; `role="option"` + `aria-selected` + `tabIndex=-1` on each item) with Esc + focus-restore via the hook (dropping the bespoke focus/Esc code); **GiftButton** (#553) â€” reuses the hook (focus the amount field, trap, Esc, restore), `aria-expanded` on the trigger, localized `aria-label` on the input; **AccentPicker** (#546) â€” the swatch `title`/`aria-label` were the raw English keys ("crimson", â€¦), now a localized `accentSwatch` string (EN + PL, other locales fall back to EN). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 testأ³w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Performance

- **Rate-limit: szybka إ›cieإ¼ka Redis (atomowy INCR) z fallbackiem do DB (audyt #453, #1 perf-finding chat-award)** â€” limiter robiإ‚ **2 zapytania Postgres** (findUnique + update/create) na kaإ¼de sprawdzenie, a chat-award sprawdza 2أ— â†’ **4 zapytania/wiadomoإ›ؤ‡** przez maإ‚y pooler. Teraz preferuje Redis (Upstash): jeden atomowy `INCR`+`PEXPIRE` przez skrypt Lua (bez wyإ›cigu incr/expire). **Bezpieczeإ„stwo zachowania:** bez Redisa â†’ إ›cieإ¼ka DB (bez zmian); bإ‚ؤ…d Redisa â†’ degradacja do **sprawdzonej إ›cieإ¼ki DB** (nie prosto do fail-open); guard ksztaإ‚tu wyniku `eval` (malformed â†’ fallback, nie liczenie na `undefined`); obie إ›cieإ¼ki fail-open na wإ‚asnym bإ‚ؤ™dzie (nigdy nie blokujؤ… legitnego ruchu). إڑcieإ¼ka DB wyodrؤ™bniona do `rateLimitDb` bez zmian logiki. Zielone: `tsc`/**234 testy**/`build` (إ›cieإ¼ka Redis aktywna tylko na prodzie z Upstash).

- **Daily-tasks: cache katalogu zadaإ„ w hot-path nagrأ³d (audyt #452)** â€” `updateDailyTaskProgress` (woإ‚ane per nagrodzona wiadomoإ›ؤ‡ czatu/Discorda) robiإ‚o `findMany` aktywnych zadaإ„ **co wywoإ‚anie**, mimo إ¼e katalog zadaإ„ jest w runtime statyczny (seedowany, إ¼adna trasa go nie mutuje). Cache listy id per `triggerType` (~5 min) + early-return gdy brak zadaإ„ danego typu (pomija pؤ™tlؤ™ upsertأ³w caإ‚kowicie) + `today()` policzony raz zamiast 3أ— w pؤ™tli. Zielone: `tsc`/**234 testy**/`build`.

- **Sezon: cache w hot-path nagrأ³d (audyt #450)** â€” `getOrCreateCurrentSeason()` robiإ‚ `updateMany` (WRITE â€‍deaktywuj wygasإ‚e") + `findUnique` na **kaإ¼de** wywoإ‚anie â€” w tym إ›cieإ¼kؤ™ nagrأ³d czatu (per wiadomoإ›ؤ‡). Sezon jest globalny (jeden wiersz/`number` miesiؤ…ca) i zmienia siؤ™ raz w miesiؤ…cu â†’ cache in-process ~5 min (jedyna nieإ›wieإ¼oإ›ؤ‡: kilka minut na przeإ‚omie miesiؤ…ca, kosmetyczna â€” XP lؤ…duje na serwowanym id sezonu); `invalidateSeasonCache()` wpiؤ™te w admin `update_season`, by edycja widaؤ‡ byإ‚o od razu. - **i18n: memoizacja zmergowanego katalogu per locale (audyt #449)** â€” `deepMerge(en, localized)` (~2200 kluczy, fallback brakujؤ…cych tإ‚umaczeإ„ do EN) liczyإ‚ siؤ™ na **kaإ¼de إ¼ؤ…danie** ZANIM cache `brandedMessages` mأ³gإ‚ zadziaإ‚aؤ‡ (cache'uje tylko wynik podmiany brandingu, nie wejإ›cie). ### Documentation

### Performance

- **Pakiet wydajnoإ›ci #2 â€” wspأ³إ‚dzielony cache overlayأ³w + agregacje DB + lإ¼ejszy polling (#443)** â€” dalsze znaleziska perf z audytu: **(1)** producery overlayأ³w owiniؤ™te w wspأ³إ‚dzielony `cacheJson` (TTL = wإ‚asny `intervalMs` feeda) â€” N إ؛rأ³deإ‚ OBS tego samego feeda dzieli **jedno** wykonanie na tick zamiast N niezaleإ¼nych pؤ™tli zapytaإ„ (Upstash miؤ™dzy instancjami serverless; viewers juإ¼ miaإ‚ wإ‚asny cache). **(2)** `pollsFeed`/`predictionsFeed` إ‚adowaإ‚y **wszystkie** gإ‚osy/zakإ‚ady co tick tylko po to, by je policzyؤ‡ â†’ `groupBy` z `_count`/`_sum` w bazie (popularna ankieta = tysiؤ…ce wierszy/tick â†’ kilka liczb). **(3)** strona `/quests` robiإ‚a **N sekwencyjnych upsertأ³w** UserTask na kaإ¼de wejإ›cie â†’ wzorzec `createMany`-tylko-brakujؤ…ce z home (typowo zero dodatkowych zapisأ³w). **(4)** `SessionProvider refetchInterval` 60s â†’ 180s â€” periodyczny pull sesji to tylko backstop (saldo i tak leci balance-busem), 3أ— mniej hitأ³w `/api/auth/session` w bazie na otwartؤ… kartؤ™. Zielone: `tsc`/**242 testy**/`build`.

### Security

- **Izolacja tenantأ³w: modele bota + globalne feedy (audyt, P0b #442)** â€” domkniؤ™cie najwyإ¼ej ocenionej luki izolacji z audytu architektury (dziإ› admin kaإ¼dego portalu edytowaإ‚ WSPأ“LNؤ„ pulؤ™): `ChatCommand`/`ChatTimer`/`FaqResponse`/`SongRequest` dostaإ‚y `tenantId` (wzorzec kolekcji: `tenantId String?`+`@@index`; `ChatCommand.trigger` z globalnego `@unique` â†’ `@@unique([tenantId, trigger])` â€” kaإ¼dy portal ma wإ‚asnؤ… przestrzeإ„ `!komend`). **db push + backfill na prod przed merge** (4 domyإ›lne komendy przypiؤ™te do foundera). Wszystkie 8 tras (admin + bot/internal) scope'owane: reads `OR [tenant, null]`, create stempluje, update/delete z owned-guardemâ†’404. Globalne feedy teإ¼ domkniؤ™te: `wheel` recent-wins i `gt-games/leaderboard` (modele user-owned) filtrowane przez `user.tenantId` â€” koniec mieszania nickأ³w graczy miؤ™dzy portalami (strona `/ranking` byإ‚a juإ¼ scopowana â€” usuniؤ™ta niespأ³jnoإ›ؤ‡). Wykonanie: schema+backfill+feedy rؤ™cznie, 8 tras agentem wg wzorca (typecheck-clean). Dla GE render 1:1. Zielone: `tsc`/**242 testy**/`build`.

### Performance

- **Pakiet wydajnoإ›ci z audytu â€” tenant memoizowany, indeksy, koniec write'أ³w co tick (#441)** â€” top-5 znalezisk perf: **(1)** `getCurrentTenant()` owiniؤ™ty w React `cache()` â€” ~6 identycznych `tenant.findUnique` na KAإ»DY render strony (metadata+viewport roota, `[locale]` layout, i18n request, stopka, page) zwija siؤ™ do **jednego**; per-request, bez TTL â†’ edycja brandingu ownera dalej dziaإ‚a natychmiast. **(2) Indeksy** (db push na prod przed merge): `transactions` miaإ‚a **ZERO** indeksأ³w mimo insertu na kaإ¼dؤ… wiadomoإ›ؤ‡ czatu â†’ `@@index([userId, createdAt])` (profil/daily-bonus) + `@@index([type, createdAt])` (ranking tygodnia/pending-orders/anomalie); `notifications` zero â†’ `[userId, createdAt]`+`[userId, read]` (dzwonek pollowany co 30-120s/usera); `admin_actions` â†’ `[createdAt]` (globalny log). **(3)** `getSettings()` (alerty) i `chatFeed` config (overlay) robiإ‚y **UPSERT/WRITE co tick SSE** (alerty co 1s, czat co 2s na kaإ¼de إ؛rأ³dإ‚o OBS) â†’ read-first (`findUnique`/defaulty), write tylko przy pierwszym czytaniu. **(4)** `lockExpiredPredictions()` odpalany co 4s/poإ‚ؤ…czenie i woإ‚ajؤ…cy `currentTenantId()` poza request-scope â†’ throttle (max raz/min/tenant) + przyjmuje request-scoped `tid` z producera SSE. **(5)** `happy-hour` cache-klucz i `botConfig` bez tenanta (przeciek konfigu miؤ™dzy portalami) â†’ `happy-hour:config:<tid>` + scoped query. Zielone: `tsc`/**242 testy**/`build`.

### Security

- **Izolacja tenantأ³w w trasach zarzؤ…dzania userami + atomowe rozstrzyganie (audyt 4-agentowy #440)** â€” przed sprzedaإ¼ؤ… white-label domkniؤ™te realne luki cross-tenant z audytu: **(1) [HIGH] eskalacja uprawnieإ„** â€” `admin/user-roles` pozwalaإ‚ adminowi portalu A nadaؤ‡ `isAdmin` userowi portalu B (lookup targetu po globalnym id/username bez tenanta); ten sam wzorzec w `grant-tokens`/`ban-user`/`deliver-order`/`merge-users` (saldo/ban/refund/scalanie cudzego portalu). Nowy helper `findManagedUser(target, gate)` w `lib/admin.ts` scope'uje cel do tenanta hosta (platform-owner dalej globalnie); `deliver-order` sprawdza `tx.user.tenantId`, `merge-users` wymaga obu kont w tenancie. `AuthResult` niesie teraz `tenantId`+`isPlatformOwner`. **(2)** `admin/assistant` miaإ‚ rؤ™czny guard bez `isWrongTenant` (mod A odpalaإ‚ AI na koszt planu B) â†’ nowy `requireAdminOrModerator()` z guardem cross-tenant. **(3) [MED] double-resolve**: `lib/duels.ts` `!accept` i `lib/predictions.ts` resolve/cancel re-guardowaإ‚y przez `findFirst` (TOCTOU pod READ COMMITTED â†’ podwأ³jna wypإ‚ata przy rأ³wnolegإ‚ym wywoإ‚aniu) â†’ atomowy claim `updateMany` z row-lockiem (`count===0` â‡’ bail) przed jakimkolwiek ruchem tokenأ³w. **(4) [LOW]** `logoUrl` tenanta (onboarding/my + admin/tenants/[id]) zapisywany bez walidacji â†’ `safeMediaUrl` (tylko http(s)). Zielone: `tsc`/**242 testy**/`build`.

- **kasyno: nowa gra DICE (koإ›ci) â€” premium tor 0-99 z animacjؤ… + fair RTP ~0.95** **(#382)** â€” pierwsza z 4 nowych gier wybranych przez usera (Dice â†’ Crash â†’ Plinko â†’ Mines). **Logika (`lib/gt-games.ts`):** `rollDice` losuje 0-99, zakإ‚ad â€‍under T" (wygrana gdy roll < T) lub â€‍over T" (roll â‰¥ T), prأ³g T = 2..98; `diceWinChance`/`diceMultiplier` â€” mnoإ¼nik = (1 âˆ’ 5% edge) / szansa â†’ **RTP ~0.95** (GT sink); `normDiceChoice` parsuje â€‍under:NN"/â€‍over:NN".
